 Abhyuthanamadharmasya tadatmanam srijamayamam means, o India, whenever religion starts to get lost and lawlessness grows, then i create myself, that is, i take birth
 maanav kii raksha, dushton ke vinaash or dharm kii punahsthapana ke liye main alag-alag yugon (kaalon) main avatarit hota hum
 So let us know about Shrihari's philosophy: 1
 matsay avatar :matsay avatar bhagwaan vishnu kaa pehla avatar he
 In this avatar, Vishnu appeared as a fish
 manyata ke anusaar ek rakshas ne jab vedon ko chura kar samudr kii gaharaai main chupa diya tha, tab bhagwaan vishnu ne matsay avatar main aakar vedon ko paaya or unhen phir sthapit kiya
 2
 varah avatar :varah avatar hindu dharm granthon ke anusaar bhagwaan vishnu ke das avtaron main se teesraa avatar he
 In this incarnation, God took the form of a pig and killed the demon Hiranyaksha
 3
 Kachhap Avatar: Kuram Avatar is also known as 'kachhap Avatar'
 isamen bhagwaan vishnu kachua banakar prakat hue the
 In the Kachhap avatar, Shri Hari handled the Mandar Parvat with his armor in the ocean of Kshirasagar
 manthan main bhagwaan vishnu, mandar parvat or vasuki sarp kii madad se devataaon or rakshason ne chaudaa ratna paae the
 4
 nrisingh bhagwaan :granthon ke anusaar bhagwaan vishnu ke das avtaron main se chauthaa avatar nrisingh hai
 In this incarnation, Lakshmipati nar-singh appeared as half lion and half human
 isamen bhagwaan kaa cheharaa sher kaa tha or sharir insaan kaa tha
 In Narsingh avatar, he killed his father Rakshasa Hiranyakashipu to protect his devotee Prahlada
 5
 Vamana Avatar: Lord Vishnu is the fifth avatar
 isamen bhagwaan bramhan balak ke rup main dharti par aae the or prahlada ke pautra raja bali se daan main teen pad dharti maangi thi
 In three steps, Vamana broke the pride of King Bali by measuring all three loks with his foot
 6
 Parashurama: Parashurama, an incarnation of Vishnu, was the son of Renuka, the daughter of King Prasenjit, and the son of Bhriguvanshi Jamadagni
 dashavataron main se vah chhathvaan avatar the
 Because of Jamadagni's son, he is also called 'jamadagnya'
 vah shiv ke param bhakt the
 Pleased with his devotion, Lord Shankar gave the Parshu weapon
 inkaa naam ram tha or parashu lene ke kaaran vah parashuram kehalaate the
 They are said to have destroyed the Kshatriyas many times
 kshatriyon ke ahamkaari vidhvansh se sansar ko bachaane ke liye inkaa janm hua tha
 7
 shriram :vishnu ke das avtaron main se ek maryaada purushottam bhagwaan shriram hai
 Maharishi Valmiki wrote the story of Rama in the Sanskrit epic Ramayana
 tulsidas ne bhakthi kavy shri ramcharitamanas kii rachana kii thi
 Rama was the son of King Dasaratha of Ayodhya and his first queen Kaushalya
 8
 Shri Krishna: Yashoda Nandan Sri Krishna was also an incarnation of Vishnu
 bhagwat granth membhagwan krishnaki lilaon kii kahaniyaan he
 He has many names like Gopal, Govind, Devaki Nandan, Vasudev, Mohan, Makhan Chor, Murari
 yah mathura main devaki or vasudev ke putr ke rup main prakat hue the
 Shri Krishna had a great role in the war of Mahabharata
 vah is yuddh main arjuna ke sarathi the
 His sister Subhadra was the wife of Arjuna
 unhone yuddh se pehle arjuna ko gita upadesh diya tha
 9
 bhagwaan buddha :bhagwaan vishnu ke dashavataron main se ek buddha bhi hai
 He is also called Gautama Buddha, Mahatma Buddha
 vah buddha dharm ke sansthaapak maane jate hai
 Buddhism is one of the four major religions of the world
 inkaa janm kshatriya kul ke shakya naresh shuddhodhan ke putr ke rup main hua tha
 He was named Siddhartha
 gautam buddha apni shaadi ke baad bachche rahul or patni yashodhara ko chhodkar sansar ko moh-maaya or dukhon se mukti dilaane ke maarg par nikal gaye the
 10
 kalki avatar :kalki avatar bhagwaan vishnu kaa aakhri avatar mana jaataa he
 According to the Kalki Purana, the 'kalki' incarnation of Shri Hari will be at the end of Kali Yuga
